

// ===== FILE: merge-all.js =====

const fs = require("fs");
const path = require("path");

const OUTPUT_FILE = "merged.txt";

const IGNORE_DIRS = [
  "node_modules",
  ".git",
  "dist",
  "build",
  "out"
];

const IGNORE_FILES = [
  OUTPUT_FILE,
  "package-lock.json"
];

const ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS = [
  ".ts",
  ".js",
  ".json",
  ".md",
];

function shouldIgnore(fullPath) {
  const parts = fullPath.split(path.sep);

  if (parts.some(part => IGNORE_DIRS.includes(part))) {
    return true;
  }

  if (IGNORE_FILES.includes(path.basename(fullPath))) {
    return true;
  }

  return false;
}

function shouldIncludeFile(fileName) {
  return ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS.some(ext =>
    fileName.endsWith(ext)
  );
}

function readDirRecursive(dir) {
  let output = "";

  const entries = fs.readdirSync(dir, { withFileTypes: true });

  for (const entry of entries) {
    const fullPath = path.join(dir, entry.name);

    if (shouldIgnore(fullPath)) continue;

    if (entry.isDirectory()) {
      output += readDirRecursive(fullPath);
    } else if (shouldIncludeFile(entry.name)) {
      output += `\n\n// ===== FILE: ${fullPath} =====\n\n`;
      output += fs.readFileSync(fullPath, "utf8");
    }
  }

  return output;
}

const mergedCode = readDirRecursive(".");
fs.writeFileSync(OUTPUT_FILE, mergedCode);

console.log("Repository merged cleanly.");

// ===== FILE: merged.js =====

// ===== FILE: README.md =====

# Cleandesk Backend
Backend service for the Cleandesk tuition-management SaaS.

## Tech Stack (v1)
  - Language: TypeScript
  - Runtime: Node.js

## Authentication (v1)

- Authentication mechanism: JWT-based token authentication
- Session model: Stateless
- Token expiry: Mandatory
- 
  Decision frozen for v1.



// ===== FILE: src\auth\auth.errors.ts =====

export class UnauthorizedError extends Error {
  statusCode = 401;

  constructor(message = 'Unauthorized') {
    super(message);
  }
}

export class ForbiddenError extends Error {
  statusCode = 403;

  constructor(message = 'Forbidden') {
    super(message);
  }
}


// ===== FILE: src\auth\auth.middleware.ts =====

import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import { buildRequestContext } from './request-context';
import { UnauthorizedError } from './auth.errors';
import { isUserSessionActive } from './session.service';

export async function requireAuth(
  req: Request,
  res: Response,
  next: NextFunction
) {
  const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;

  if (!authHeader) {
    throw new UnauthorizedError('Authorization token missing');
  }

  const [scheme, token] = authHeader.split(' ');

  if (scheme !== 'Bearer' || !token) {
    throw new UnauthorizedError('Invalid authorization format');
  }

  try {
    const context = buildRequestContext(token);

    const isSessionActive = await isUserSessionActive({
      sessionId: context.session_id,
      userId: context.user_id,
    });

    if (!isSessionActive) {
      throw new UnauthorizedError('Invalid or expired token');
    }

    // Attach context to request
    (req as any).context = context;

    next();
  } catch (err) {
    throw new UnauthorizedError('Invalid or expired token');
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\auth\auth.service.ts =====

import { pool } from "../db/db";
import { comparePassword } from "../security/password";
import { RoleId } from "./roles";

type AuthResult = {
  user_id: string;
  role_id: RoleId;
  institute_id: string;
};

export async function authenticateUser(
  loginIdentifier: string,
  password: string
): Promise<AuthResult | null> {
  const query = `
    SELECT
      id,
      role_id,
      institute_id,
      password_hash,
      is_active
    FROM "user"
    WHERE login_identifier = $1
    LIMIT 1
  `;

  const result = await pool.query(query, [loginIdentifier]);

  // User not found
  if (result.rowCount === 0) {
    return null;
  }

  const user = result.rows[0];

  // Inactive user
  if (!user.is_active) {
    return null;
  }

  // Password check
  const passwordOk = await comparePassword(
    password,
    user.password_hash
  );

  if (!passwordOk) {
    return null;
  }

  // Success: identity only
  return {
    user_id: user.id,
    role_id: user.role_id as RoleId,
    institute_id: user.institute_id,
  };
}

import { ROLES } from './roles';
import { ForbiddenError } from './auth.errors';

throw new ForbiddenError('Students cannot modify system state');
  }
}


// ===== FILE: src\auth\login-identifier.service.ts =====

import { randomUUID } from "crypto";

/**
 * Deterministic v1 rule:
 * login_identifier = <rolePrefix>-<shortUUID>
 *
 * Example:
 * ADM-a82f1c2d
 * TCH-9bc120ef
 *
 * This guarantees:
 * - Backend controlled
 * - Practically collision-free (UUID based)
 * - Role traceable
 */
export function generateLoginIdentifier(roleId: number): string {
  const rolePrefixMap: Record<number, string> = {
    1: "ADM",
    2: "MGT",
    3: "TCH",
    4: "STD",
  };

  const prefix = rolePrefixMap[roleId];

  if (!prefix) {
    throw new Error("Invalid role for login identifier generation");
  }

  const shortId = randomUUID().split("-")[0];

  return `${prefix}-${shortId}`;
}


// ===== FILE: src\auth\refresh-token.service.ts =====

// src/auth/refresh-token.service.ts

import { pool } from "../db/db";
import { randomBytes, createHash } from "crypto";

function hashToken(tokenValue: string): string {
  return createHash("sha256").update(tokenValue).digest("hex");
}

const REFRESH_TOKEN_BYTES = 48;
const REFRESH_TOKEN_TTL_DAYS = 30;
const REFRESH_TOKEN_ABSOLUTE_TTL_DAYS = 90; // max session regardless of activity

export function generateRefreshTokenValue(): string {
  return randomBytes(REFRESH_TOKEN_BYTES).toString("hex");
}

export function getRefreshTokenExpiry(referenceDate = new Date()): Date {
  const d = new Date(referenceDate);
  d.setDate(d.getDate() + REFRESH_TOKEN_TTL_DAYS);
  return d;
}

export function getRefreshTokenAbsoluteExpiry(referenceDate: Date): Date {
  const d = new Date(referenceDate);
  d.setDate(d.getDate() + REFRESH_TOKEN_ABSOLUTE_TTL_DAYS);
  return d;
}

/**
 * Creates a refresh token record linked to a session family.
 * familyId groups all rotated tokens for a single login event.
 * If familyId is null, a new family is started (first login).
 */
export async function createRefreshToken(input: {
  userId: string;
  sessionId: string;
  familyId: string | null;
  absoluteExpiresAt: Date;
}): Promise<{ tokenValue: string; expiresAt: Date }> {
  const tokenValue = generateRefreshTokenValue();
  const expiresAt = getRefreshTokenExpiry();

  const familyId = input.familyId ?? tokenValue.slice(0, 16); // use first 16 chars as family seed

  await pool.query(
    `INSERT INTO refresh_token (
      token_hash,
      user_id,
      session_id,
      family_id,
      expires_at,
      absolute_expires_at,
      created_at
    )
    VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, NOW())`,
    [
      hashToken(tokenValue),
      input.userId,
      input.sessionId,
      familyId,
      expiresAt,
      input.absoluteExpiresAt,
    ]
  );

  return { tokenValue, expiresAt };
}

export type RefreshTokenRow = {
  token_hash: string;
  user_id: string;
  session_id: string;
  family_id: string;
  expires_at: Date;
  absolute_expires_at: Date;
  revoked_at: Date | null;
  used_at: Date | null;
};

/**
 * Looks up a refresh token by value (hashed on lookup).
 * Returns null if not found.
 */
export async function findRefreshToken(
  tokenValue: string
): Promise<RefreshTokenRow | null> {
  const result = await pool.query<RefreshTokenRow>(
    `SELECT
       token_hash, user_id, session_id, family_id,
       expires_at, absolute_expires_at, revoked_at, used_at
     FROM refresh_token
     WHERE token_hash = $1
     LIMIT 1`,
    [hashToken(tokenValue)]
  );

  return result.rows[0] ?? null;
}

/**
 * Marks a refresh token as used and creates a new rotated one.
 * Returns the new token value.
 * 
 * SECURITY: If the token has already been used (used_at IS NOT NULL),
 * we detect a replay attack — revoke the entire family immediately.
 */
export async function rotateRefreshToken(
  tokenValue: string
): Promise<{
  newTokenValue: string;
  newExpiresAt: Date;
  userId: string;
  sessionId: string;
} | null> {
  const client = await pool.connect();
  try {
    await client.query("BEGIN");

    // Lock the row for update
    const result = await client.query<RefreshTokenRow>(
      `SELECT
         token_hash, user_id, session_id, family_id,
         expires_at, absolute_expires_at, revoked_at, used_at
       FROM refresh_token
       WHERE token_hash = $1
       FOR UPDATE`,
      [hashToken(tokenValue)]
    );

    const token = result.rows[0];

    if (!token) {
      await client.query("ROLLBACK");
      return null;
    }

    // REPLAY ATTACK DETECTION: token already used → revoke entire family
    if (token.used_at !== null) {
      await client.query(
        `UPDATE refresh_token
         SET revoked_at = NOW()
         WHERE family_id = $1
           AND revoked_at IS NULL`,
        [token.family_id]
      );
      // Also revoke the user session
      await client.query(
        `UPDATE user_session
         SET revoked_at = NOW()
         WHERE id = $1 AND revoked_at IS NULL`,
        [token.session_id]
      );
      await client.query("COMMIT");
      return null;
    }

    // Token is revoked or expired
    if (
      token.revoked_at !== null ||
      new Date() > token.expires_at ||
      new Date() > token.absolute_expires_at
    ) {
      await client.query("ROLLBACK");
      return null;
    }

    // Mark old token as used (not revoked yet — used + rotation creates the new one)
    await client.query(
      `UPDATE refresh_token
       SET used_at = NOW()
       WHERE token_hash = $1`,
      [hashToken(tokenValue)]
    );

    // Issue new token in the same family, same absolute expiry
    const newTokenValue = generateRefreshTokenValue();
    const newExpiresAt = getRefreshTokenExpiry();

    await client.query(
      `INSERT INTO refresh_token (
         token_hash, user_id, session_id, family_id,
         expires_at, absolute_expires_at, created_at
       )
       VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, NOW())`,
      [
        hashToken(newTokenValue),
        token.user_id,
        token.session_id,
        token.family_id,
        newExpiresAt,
        token.absolute_expires_at,
      ]
    );

    // Slide the user_session expiry to match new refresh token
    await client.query(
      `UPDATE user_session
       SET expires_at = $1
       WHERE id = $2 AND revoked_at IS NULL`,
      [newExpiresAt, token.session_id]
    );

    await client.query("COMMIT");

    return {
      newTokenValue,
      newExpiresAt,
      userId: token.user_id,
      sessionId: token.session_id,
    };
  } catch (err) {
    await client.query("ROLLBACK");
    throw err;
  } finally {
    client.release();
  }
}

/**
 * Revokes all refresh tokens for a session (logout).
 */
export async function revokeRefreshTokensForSession(
  sessionId: string
): Promise<void> {
  await pool.query(
    `UPDATE refresh_token
     SET revoked_at = NOW()
     WHERE session_id = $1
       AND revoked_at IS NULL`,
    [sessionId]
  );
}

/**
 * Revokes all refresh tokens for a user across all sessions (force logout all devices).
 */
export async function revokeAllRefreshTokensForUser(
  userId: string
): Promise<void> {
  await pool.query(
    `UPDATE refresh_token
     SET revoked_at = NOW()
     WHERE user_id = $1
       AND revoked_at IS NULL`,
    [userId]
  );
}

// ===== FILE: src\auth\request-context.ts =====

import { RoleId, type Role } from './roles';
import { verifyToken } from './token.service';

export function buildRequestContext(token: string): RequestContext {
  const payload = verifyToken(token);

  return {
    user_id: payload.user_id,
    role_id: payload.role_id,
    institute_id: payload.institute_id,
    session_id: payload.session_id,
  };
}

export type RequestContext = {
  user_id: string;
  role_id: RoleId;
  institute_id: string;
  session_id: string;
};

declare global {
  namespace Express {
    interface User {
      id: string;
      role: Role;
      instituteId: string;
    }

    interface Request {
      user?: User;
    }
  }
}

export {};

// ===== FILE: src\auth\require-institute-inheritence.ts =====

import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from "express";
import { assertNoInstituteInRequest } from "./user-institute.policy";

export function requireInstituteInheritance(
  req: Request,
  res: Response,
  next: NextFunction
) {
  if (!req.context) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: "Unauthenticated" });
  }

  try {
    assertNoInstituteInRequest(req.body);
  } catch (err) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      error: "Institute assignment is not allowed",
    });
  }

  /**
   * Attach inherited institute explicitly for downstream use.
   * Controller/service MUST use this value, not req.body.
   */
  (req as Request & { inheritedInstituteId: string }).inheritedInstituteId =
    req.context.institute_id;
  next();
}


// ===== FILE: src\auth\require-role.ts =====

import { RequestContext } from './request-context';
import { RoleId } from './roles';
import { ForbiddenError } from './auth.errors';


export function requireRole(
  context: RequestContext,
  allowedRoles: RoleId[]
): void {
  if (!allowedRoles.includes(context.role_id)) {
throw new ForbiddenError('Insufficient role');
  }
}



// ===== FILE: src\auth\require-user-creation-authorization.ts =====

import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from "express";
import { canCreateRole } from "./user-creation.policy";
import { ROLES, type Role } from "./roles";

export function requireUserCreationAuthorization(
  req: Request,
  res: Response,
  next: NextFunction
) {
  const context = (req as any).context;

  if (!context) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: "Unauthenticated" });
  }

  const rawRole = req.body.role;

  if (typeof rawRole !== "number") {
    return res.status(400).json({
      error: "Role must be a numeric role_id",
    });
  }

  // Type guard
  function isValidRole(role: number): role is Role {
    return Object.values(ROLES).includes(role as Role);
  }

  if (!isValidRole(rawRole)) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      error: "Invalid role",
    });
  }

  const targetRole = rawRole; // now narrowed to Role

  if (!canCreateRole(context.role_id, targetRole)) {
    return res.status(403).json({
      error: "You are not allowed to create this role",
    });
  }

  next();
}

// ===== FILE: src\auth\roles.ts =====

export const ROLES = {
  ADMIN: 1,
  MANAGEMENT: 2,
  TEACHER: 3,
  STUDENT: 4,
} as const;

export type RoleId = typeof ROLES[keyof typeof ROLES];
export type Role = typeof ROLES[keyof typeof ROLES];


// ===== FILE: src\auth\session.service.ts =====

import { pool } from '../db/db';

export async function createUserSession(input: {
  sessionId: string;
  userId: string;
  expiresAt: Date;
}): Promise<void> {
  await pool.query(
    `INSERT INTO public.user_session (
      id,
      user_id,
      expires_at
    ) VALUES ($1, $2, $3)`,
    [input.sessionId, input.userId, input.expiresAt]
  );
}

export async function isUserSessionActive(input: {
  sessionId: string;
  userId: string;
}): Promise<boolean> {
  const result = await pool.query(
    `SELECT 1
     FROM public.user_session
     WHERE id = $1
       AND user_id = $2
       AND revoked_at IS NULL
       AND expires_at > now()
     LIMIT 1`,
    [input.sessionId, input.userId]
  );

  return Number(result.rowCount ?? 0) > 0;
}

export async function revokeUserSession(input: {
  sessionId: string;
  userId: string;
}): Promise<void> {
  await pool.query(
    `UPDATE public.user_session
     SET revoked_at = now()
     WHERE id = $1
       AND user_id = $2
       AND revoked_at IS NULL`,
    [input.sessionId, input.userId]
  );
}

// ===== FILE: src\auth\token.service.ts =====

import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';
import { randomUUID } from 'crypto';
import { RoleId } from './roles';

function getJwtSecret(): string {
  const secret = process.env.JWT_SECRET;

  if (!secret) {
    throw new Error('JWT_SECRET is not set');
  }

  return secret;
}

export type TokenPayload = {
  user_id: string;
  role_id: RoleId;
  institute_id: string;
  session_id: string;
};

const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET;

if (!JWT_SECRET) {
  throw new Error('JWT_SECRET is not set');
}

const JWT_EXPIRY = '15m';
const JWT_EXPIRY_MS = 15 * 60 * 1000;

export function createSessionId(): string {
  return randomUUID();
}

export function getTokenExpiryDate(referenceDate = new Date()): Date {
  return new Date(referenceDate.getTime() + JWT_EXPIRY_MS);
}

export function generateToken(payload: TokenPayload): string {
  return jwt.sign(
    {
      user_id: payload.user_id,
      role_id: payload.role_id,
      institute_id: payload.institute_id,
      session_id: payload.session_id,
    },
    getJwtSecret(),
    {
      expiresIn: JWT_EXPIRY,
    }
  );
}

export function verifyToken(token: string): TokenPayload {
  try {
    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, getJwtSecret());

    // jwt.verify returns string | object
    if (typeof decoded !== 'object' || decoded === null) {
      throw new Error('Invalid token payload');
    }

    const payload = decoded as TokenPayload;

    // Minimal structural validation (no trust yet)
    if (
      !payload.user_id ||
      !payload.role_id ||
      !payload.institute_id ||
      !payload.session_id
    ) {
      throw new Error('Token payload missing required fields');
    }

    return payload;
  } catch (err) {
    throw new Error('Invalid or expired token');
  }
}


// ===== FILE: src\auth\user-creation.policy.ts =====

import { ROLES, type Role } from "./roles";

/**
 * Defines which roles are allowed to create which other roles.
 * This is a HARD SECURITY POLICY.
 */
const ALLOWED_CREATION_MAP: Record<Role, Role[]> = {
  [ROLES.ADMIN]: [ROLES.MANAGEMENT, ROLES.TEACHER, ROLES.STUDENT],
  [ROLES.MANAGEMENT]: [ROLES.TEACHER, ROLES.STUDENT],
  [ROLES.TEACHER]: [],
  [ROLES.STUDENT]: [],
};

export function canCreateRole(
  creatorRole: Role,
  targetRole: Role
): boolean {
  const allowedTargets = ALLOWED_CREATION_MAP[creatorRole];

  if (!allowedTargets) return false;

  return allowedTargets.includes(targetRole);
}


// ===== FILE: src\auth\user-institute.policy.ts =====

/**
 * HARD INVARIANT:
 * A user being created must inherit the institute of the authenticated creator.
 * The client is never allowed to choose or override institute_id.
 */

export function assertNoInstituteInRequest(body: unknown): void {
  if (
    typeof body === "object" &&
    body !== null &&
    "instituteId" in body
  ) {
    throw new Error("instituteId must not be provided by client");
  }
}


// ===== FILE: src\controllers\academic-year-activate.controller.ts =====

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { activateAcademicYear } from "../services/academic-year-activate.service";

type ActivateParams = {
  academicYearId: string;
};

export async function activateAcademicYearController(
  req: Request<ActivateParams>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN]);

  try {
    const { academicYearId } = req.params;

    const result = await activateAcademicYear({
      academicYearId,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({
      success: true,
      data: result,
    });

  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\controllers\academic-year.controller.ts =====

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { createAcademicYear } from "../services/academic-year-create.service";
import { listAcademicYears } from "../services/academic-year-list.service";
import { updateAcademicYear } from "../services/academic-year-update.service";

export async function createAcademicYearController(
  req: Request,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  // 🔐 MA-01 enforcement
  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN]);

  try {
    const { label } = req.body;

    if (!label) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        error: "Academic year label is required",
      });
    }

    const academicYear = await createAcademicYear({
      label,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
    });

    return res.status(201).json({
      success: true,
      data: academicYear,
    });

  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,

      
    });
  }
}

export async function updateAcademicYearController(
  req: Request<{ academicYearId: string }>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN]);

  try {
    const { academicYearId } = req.params;
    const { label } = req.body;

    if (!label || typeof label !== "string" || !label.trim()) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        success: false,
        error: "Academic year label is required",
      });
    }

    const updated = await updateAcademicYear({
      academicYearId,
      label: label.trim(),
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({
      success: true,
      data: updated,
    });

  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}


export async function listAcademicYearsController(

) {

      total_alumni,
    });

  } catch (err: any) {

      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\controllers\announcement.controller.ts =====

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { createAnnouncement } from "../services/announcement-create.service";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { denyStudentMutation } from "../auth/deny-student";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { updateAnnouncement } from "../services/announcement-update.service";
import { listAnnouncements } from "../services/announcement-list.service";

type UpdateAnnouncementParams = {
  announcementId: string;
};

export async function createAnnouncementController(
  req: Request,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  // 🔐 Role enforcement (MA-011 / MA-012 / MA-013 / MA-014)
  requireRole(context, [
    ROLES.ADMIN,
    ROLES.MANAGEMENT,
    ROLES.TEACHER,
  ]);

  // 🚫 Absolute student mutation block
  denyStudentMutation(context);

  try {
    const {
      announcement_type,
      announcement_title,
      message,
      class_batch_id,
      school_attribute,
    } = req.body;

    const announcement = await createAnnouncement({
      announcementType: announcement_type,
      announcementTitle: announcement_title,
      message,
      classBatchId: class_batch_id ?? null,
      schoolAttribute: school_attribute ?? null,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
    });

    return res.status(201).json({
      success: true,
      data: announcement,
    });

  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}


export async function updateAnnouncementController(
  req: Request<UpdateAnnouncementParams>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  // 🔐 MA-015 role enforcement
  requireRole(context, [
    ROLES.ADMIN,
    ROLES.MANAGEMENT,
    ROLES.TEACHER,
  ]);

  // 🚫 Students cannot mutate
  denyStudentMutation(context);

  try {
    const { announcementId } = req.params;

    const {
      announcement_title,
      message,
      school_attribute,
      is_active,
    } = req.body;

    const updated = await updateAnnouncement({
      announcementId,
      announcementTitle: announcement_title,
      message,
      schoolAttribute: school_attribute,
      isActive: is_active,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({
      success: true,
      data: updated,
    });

  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\controllers\attendance-summary.controller.ts =====

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { getAttendanceSummary } from "../services/attendance-summary.service";
import { getAppLocalDate } from "../utils/app-date";

export async function getAttendanceSummaryController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;
  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);

  const date = (req.query.date as string) || getAppLocalDate();

  if (!/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(date)) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "Invalid date format. Use YYYY-MM-DD." });
  }

  try {
    const result = await getAttendanceSummary(context.institute_id, date);
    return res.status(200).json({
      date,
      rows: result.rows,
      holiday: result.holiday,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("[attendance-summary] Error:", err?.message ?? err);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: "Failed to fetch attendance summary" });
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\controllers\attendance.controller.ts =====

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { createAttendanceRecord } from "../Modules/Attendance/attendance-create.service";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { denyStudentMutation } from "../auth/deny-student";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { updateAttendanceRecord } from "../services/attendance-update.service";
import { getAttendanceHistoryService } from "../services/attendance-history.service";
import { getPendingAttendanceService } from "../services/attendance-pending.service";
import { getAttendanceBatchSummary } from "../services/attendance-batch-summary.service";
import { getAttendanceBatchDetail } from "../services/attendance-batch-detail.service";
import { getStudentAttendancePageService } from "../services/student-attendance-page.service";

type UpdateAttendanceParams = {
  attendanceId: string;
};

type GetAttendanceHistoryParams = {
  studentId: string;
};

export async function createAttendanceController(
  req: Request,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [
    ROLES.ADMIN,
    ROLES.MANAGEMENT,
    ROLES.TEACHER,
  ]);

  denyStudentMutation(context);

  try {
    const {
      student_id,
      class_batch_id,
      attendance_date,
      status,
      late,
      early_leave,
    } = req.body;

    const record = await createAttendanceRecord({
      studentId: student_id,
      classBatchId: class_batch_id,
      attendanceDate: attendance_date,
      status,
      late,
      earlyLeave: early_leave,
      markedBy: context.user_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
    });

    return res.status(201).json({
      success: true,
      data: record,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}

export async function updateAttendanceController(
  req: Request<UpdateAttendanceParams>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [
    ROLES.ADMIN,
    ROLES.MANAGEMENT,
    ROLES.TEACHER,
  ]);

  denyStudentMutation(context);

  try {
    const { attendanceId } = req.params;
    const { status, late, early_leave } = req.body;

    const updated = await updateAttendanceRecord({
      attendanceId,
      status,
      late,
      earlyLeave: early_leave,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({
      success: true,
      data: updated,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}

export async function getAttendanceHistoryController(
  req: Request<GetAttendanceHistoryParams>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;
  const studentId = req.params.studentId;

  try {
    if (context.role_id === ROLES.STUDENT) {
      if (context.user_id !== studentId) {
        return res.status(403).json({
          error: "Students can view only their own attendance",
        });
      }
    }

    const history = await getAttendanceHistoryService({
      studentId,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({
      success: true,
      data: history,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}

export async function getStudentAttendancePageController(
  req: Request,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  if (context.role_id !== ROLES.STUDENT) {
    return res.status(403).json({ success: false, error: "Access denied" });
  }

  try {
    const payload = await getStudentAttendancePageService({
      studentId: context.user_id,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: payload });
  } catch (err: any) {
    const status = err.statusCode ?? 500;
    return res.status(status).json({ success: false, error: err.message ?? "Failed to fetch attendance" });
  }
}

  }
}

      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,

// ===== FILE: src\controllers\dashboard.controller.ts =====

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { getDashboardSummary } from "../services/dashboard.service";
import {
  getTeacherDashboardSummary,
  getTeacherUpcomingTests,
  getTeacherBatches,
} from "../services/teacher-dashboard.service";
import { calcAttendancePct } from "../utils/calculations";

export async function getAdminDashboardSummaryController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;
  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);

  try {
    const row = await getDashboardSummary(context.institute_id);

    if (!row) {
      return res.status(200).json({
        summary: {
          total_students: 0,
          new_this_week: 0,
          active_batches: 0,
          upcoming_tests: 0,
          attendance_today_pct: null,
          attendance_marked_present: 0,
          attendance_total_marked: 0,
          is_holiday_today: false,
          holiday_name: null,
        },
      });
    }

    const attendancePct = row.is_holiday_today
      ? null
      : calcAttendancePct(row.marked_present, row.total_marked);

    return res.status(200).json({
      summary: {
        total_students: row.total_students,
        new_this_week: row.new_this_week,
        active_batches: row.active_batches,
        upcoming_tests: row.upcoming_tests,
        attendance_today_pct: attendancePct,
        attendance_marked_present: row.marked_present,
        attendance_total_marked: row.total_marked,
        is_holiday_today: row.is_holiday_today,
        holiday_name: row.holiday_name,
      },
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("[dashboard-summary] Error:", err?.message ?? err);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: "Failed to fetch dashboard summary" });
  }
}

export async function getTeacherDashboardSummaryController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;
  requireRole(context, [ROLES.TEACHER]);

  try {
    const summary = await getTeacherDashboardSummary(context.user_id, context.institute_id);
    return res.status(200).json({ summary });
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("[teacher-dashboard-summary] Error:", err?.message ?? err);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: "Failed to fetch teacher dashboard summary" });
  }
}

export async function getTeacherDashboardUpcomingTestsController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;
  requireRole(context, [ROLES.TEACHER]);

  const limit = Math.min(parseInt((req.query.limit as string) || "5", 10), 20);

  try {
    const tests = await getTeacherUpcomingTests(context.user_id, context.institute_id, limit);
    return res.status(200).json({ tests });
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("[teacher-dashboard-upcoming-tests] Error:", err?.message ?? err);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: "Failed to fetch upcoming tests" });
  }
}

export async function getTeacherDashboardBatchesController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;
  requireRole(context, [ROLES.TEACHER]);

  try {
    const batches = await getTeacherBatches(context.user_id, context.institute_id);
    return res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: batches, batches });
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("[teacher-dashboard-batches] Error:", err?.message ?? err);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: "Failed to fetch teacher batches" });
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\controllers\fee-structure.controller.ts =====

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { createFeeStructure } from "../services/fee-structure-create.service";
import { deactivateFeeStructure } from "../services/fee-structure-deactivate.service";
import { getFeeStructureForBatch } from "../services/fee-structure-read.service";

export async function createFeeStructureController(
  req: Request,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN]);

  try {
    const {
      class_batch_id,
      label,
      total_amount,
      lump_sum_enabled,
      installments_enabled,
      lump_sum_discount,
      final_due_date,
      late_fee_amount,
      late_fee_type,
      require_advance,
      installments,
    } = req.body;

    if (!class_batch_id || typeof class_batch_id !== "string") {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "class_batch_id is required" });
    }
    if (!label || typeof label !== "string" || !label.trim()) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "label is required" });
    }
    if (total_amount == null || isNaN(Number(total_amount))) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "total_amount is required and must be a number" });
    }
    if (lump_sum_enabled == null || installments_enabled == null) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "lump_sum_enabled and installments_enabled are required" });
    }
    if (!final_due_date) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "final_due_date is required" });
    }

    const result = await createFeeStructure({
      classBatchId: class_batch_id,
      label: label.trim(),
      totalAmount: Number(total_amount),
      lumpSumEnabled: Boolean(lump_sum_enabled),
      installmentsEnabled: Boolean(installments_enabled),
      lumpSumDiscount: lump_sum_discount != null ? Number(lump_sum_discount) : null,
      finalDueDate: final_due_date,
      lateFeeAmount: late_fee_amount != null ? Number(late_fee_amount) : null,
      lateFeeType: late_fee_type ?? null,
      requireAdvance: require_advance ?? false,
      installments: installments ?? [],
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
    });

    return res.status(201).json({
      success: true,
      data: result,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    const status = err.statusCode ?? 400;
    return res.status(status).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}

export async function deactivateFeeStructureController(
  req: Request<{ id: string }>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN]);

  try {
    const { id } = req.params;

    if (!id || typeof id !== "string") {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "Fee structure ID is required" });
    }

    await deactivateFeeStructure({
      feeStructureId: id,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
  } catch (err: any) {
    const status = err.statusCode ?? 400;
    return res.status(status).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}


export async function getFeeStructureForBatchController(
  req: Request<{ batchId: string }>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);

  try {
    const { batchId } = req.params;

    if (!batchId || typeof batchId !== "string") {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "batchId is required" });
    }

    const structure = await getFeeStructureForBatch({
      classBatchId: batchId,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({
      success: true,
      data: structure, // null when no active structure exists - per spec
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    const status = err.statusCode ?? 400;
    return res.status(status).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\controllers\holiday.controller.ts =====

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { denyStudentMutation } from "../auth/deny-student";
import { createHoliday } from "../services/holiday-create.service";
import { getHolidayForDate } from "../services/holiday-check.service";
import { cancelHoliday } from "../services/holiday-cancel.service";

export async function createHolidayController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);
  denyStudentMutation(context);

  try {
    const { holiday_date, name, class_batch_id } = req.body;

    if (!holiday_date || !/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(holiday_date)) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        success: false,
        error: "holiday_date is required in YYYY-MM-DD format",
      });
    }

    const holiday = await createHoliday({
      holidayDate: holiday_date,
      name: String(name ?? ""),
      classBatchId: class_batch_id ?? null,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
    });

    return res.status(201).json({
      success: true,
      data: holiday,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    const status = err.statusCode ?? 400;
    return res.status(status).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}

export async function getHolidayStatusController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;

  try {
    const date = req.query.date as string;
    const classBatchId = (req.query.class_batch_id as string) ?? null;

    if (!date || !/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(date)) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        success: false,
        error: "date query param required (YYYY-MM-DD)",
      });
    }

    const holiday = await getHolidayForDate({
      instituteId: context.institute_id,
      date,
      classBatchId,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({
      success: true,
      data: {
        is_holiday: holiday !== null,
        holiday,
      },
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}


export async function cancelHolidayController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);
  denyStudentMutation(context);

  try {
    const id = Array.isArray(req.params.id) ? req.params.id[0] : req.params.id;

    if (!id) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "Holiday ID is required" });
    }

    await cancelHoliday({
      holidayId: id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
  } catch (err: any) {
    const status = err.statusCode ?? 400;
    return res.status(status).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
  }
}

import { listHolidays, getActiveHolidaysForDate } from "../services/holiday-list.service";

export async function listHolidaysController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;

  // All authenticated roles can see the holiday list (students need it for attendance view)
  try {
    const upcomingOnly = req.query.upcoming === "true";
    const limit = req.query.limit ? Math.min(Number(req.query.limit), 500) : 100;
    const forDate = req.query.date as string | undefined;

    // If a specific date is requested, return all active holidays for that date
    // (used by attendance page to know which batches already have holiday declared)
    if (forDate) {
      if (!/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(forDate)) {
        return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "date must be YYYY-MM-DD" });
      }
      const holidays = await getActiveHolidaysForDate(context.institute_id, forDate);
      return res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: holidays });
    }

    const holidays = await listHolidays(context.institute_id, { upcomingOnly, limit });

    return res.status(200).json({
      success: true,
      data: holidays,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\controllers\list-teachers.controller.ts =====

// src/controllers/list-teachers.controller.ts

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { pool } from "../db/db";

export async function listTeachersController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);

  try {
    const result = await pool.query(
      `SELECT
         u.id,
         u.login_identifier,
         u.is_active,
         u.created_at,
         up.full_name,
         up.mobile,
         up.email,
         COALESCE(
           json_agg(
             json_build_object(
               'id',      cb.id,
               'name',    cb.name,
               'subject', tcb.subject
             ) ORDER BY cb.name
           ) FILTER (WHERE cb.id IS NOT NULL),
           '[]'
         ) AS assigned_batches
       FROM "user" u
       JOIN user_profile up ON up.user_id = u.id
       JOIN teacher t ON t.user_id = u.id
       LEFT JOIN teacher_class_batch tcb ON tcb.teacher_user_id = u.id
       LEFT JOIN class_batch cb ON cb.id = tcb.class_batch_id AND cb.is_active = true
       WHERE u.institute_id = $1
         AND u.role_id = $2
       GROUP BY u.id, u.login_identifier, u.is_active, u.created_at,
                up.full_name, up.mobile, up.email
       ORDER BY up.full_name ASC`,
      [context.institute_id, ROLES.TEACHER]
    );

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: result.rows });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
  }
}

    const limit      = Math.min(parseInt((req.query.limit as string) ?? "20", 10), 100);

      userId:      context.user_id,

    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: "Failed to fetch notifications" });
  }

export async function markNotificationsReadController(

      ? req.body.notification_ids
      : undefined;

      instituteId:     context.institute_id,
      notificationIds: ids,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("[notifications-mark-read] Error:", err?.message ?? err);
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: "Failed to mark notifications read" });
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\controllers\payment.controller.ts =====

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { recordPayment } from "../services/payment-create.service";
import { cancelPayment } from "../services/payment-cancel.service";
import { listPaymentsForFeeRecord } from "../services/payment-list.service";

export async function recordPaymentController(
  req: Request<{ studentFeeRecordId: string }>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);

  try {
    const { studentFeeRecordId } = req.params;

    if (!studentFeeRecordId || typeof studentFeeRecordId !== "string") {
      return res.status(400).json({
        success: false,
        error: "studentFeeRecordId is required",
      });
    }

    const {
      amount,
      payment_date,
      payment_mode,
      payment_reference,
      note,
      installment_plan_id,
    } = req.body;

    if (amount == null || isNaN(Number(amount))) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        success: false,
        error: "amount is required and must be a number",
      });
    }

    if (!payment_date) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        success: false,
        error: "payment_date is required",
      });
    }

    if (!payment_mode) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        success: false,
        error: "payment_mode is required",
      });
    }

    const payment = await recordPayment({
      studentFeeRecordId,
      amount: Number(amount),
      paymentDate: payment_date,
      paymentMode: payment_mode,
      paymentReference: payment_reference ?? null,
      note: note ?? null,
      installmentPlanId: installment_plan_id ?? null,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
    });

    return res.status(201).json({
      success: true,
      data: payment,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    const status = err.statusCode ?? 400;
    return res.status(status).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}export async function cancelPaymentController(
  req: Request<{ paymentId: string }>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);

  try {
    const { paymentId } = req.params;

    if (!paymentId || typeof paymentId !== "string") {
      return res.status(400).json({
        success: false,
        error: "paymentId is required",
      });
    }

    const { cancellation_reason } = req.body;

    if (
      !cancellation_reason ||
      typeof cancellation_reason !== "string" ||
      !cancellation_reason.trim()
    ) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        success: false,
        error: "cancellation_reason is required",
      });
    }

    await cancelPayment({
      paymentId,
      cancellationReason: cancellation_reason,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
  } catch (err: any) {
    const status = err.statusCode ?? 400;
    return res.status(status).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}export async function listPaymentsController(
  req: Request<{ studentFeeRecordId: string }>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);

  try {
    const { studentFeeRecordId } = req.params;

    if (!studentFeeRecordId || typeof studentFeeRecordId !== "string") {
      return res.status(400).json({
        success: false,
        error: "studentFeeRecordId is required",
      });
    }

    const includesCancelled = req.query.include_cancelled === "true";

    const result = await listPaymentsForFeeRecord({
      studentFeeRecordId,
      includesCancelled,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({
      success: true,
      data: result,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    const status = err.statusCode ?? 400;
    return res.status(status).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\controllers\profile.controller.ts =====

// src/controllers/profile.controller.ts

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { pool } from "../db/db";

export async function getMyProfileController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;
  const userId = context.user_id;
  const instituteId = context.institute_id;

  try {
    const result = await pool.query(
      `SELECT
         up.full_name,
         up.email,
         up.mobile,
         up.address,
         up.created_at,
         i.name AS institute_name
       FROM user_profile up
       JOIN "user" u ON u.id = up.user_id
       JOIN institute i ON i.id = u.institute_id
       WHERE up.user_id = $1
         AND u.institute_id = $2
         AND u.is_active = true`,
      [userId, instituteId]
    );

    if (result.rowCount === 0) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Profile not found" });
    }

    return res.status(200).json({ profile: result.rows[0] });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(500).json({ error: "Failed to fetch profile" });
  }
}
export async function updateMyProfileController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;
  const userId = context.user_id;
  const instituteId = context.institute_id;

  try {
    const { full_name, email, mobile, address } = req.body;

    // Build SET clause dynamically — only update fields that were sent
    const updates: string[] = [];
    const values: any[] = [];
    let idx = 1;

    if (full_name !== undefined) {
      const trimmed = String(full_name).trim();
      if (!trimmed) return res.status(400).json({ error: "Full name cannot be empty" });
      updates.push(`full_name = $${idx++}`);
      values.push(trimmed);
    }
    if (email !== undefined) {
      updates.push(`email = $${idx++}`);
      values.push(email === "" ? null : String(email).trim());
    }
    if (mobile !== undefined) {
      updates.push(`mobile = $${idx++}`);
      values.push(mobile === "" ? null : String(mobile).trim());
    }
    if (address !== undefined) {
      updates.push(`address = $${idx++}`);
      values.push(address === "" ? null : String(address).trim());
    }

    if (updates.length === 0) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: "No fields provided to update" });
    }

    // Verify user belongs to this institute before updating
    values.push(userId);
    values.push(instituteId);

    await pool.query(
      `UPDATE user_profile up
       SET ${updates.join(", ")}
       FROM "user" u
       WHERE up.user_id = u.id
         AND u.id = $${idx++}
         AND u.institute_id = $${idx++}
         AND u.is_active = true`,
      values
    );

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(500).json({ error: "Failed to update profile" });
  }
}

export async function changePasswordController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;
  const userId = context.user_id;

  try {
    const { current_password, new_password } = req.body;

    if (!current_password || !new_password) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: "current_password and new_password are required" });
    }

    if (typeof new_password !== "string" || new_password.length < 8) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: "New password must be at least 8 characters" });
    }

    // 1. Fetch current password hash
    const userResult = await pool.query(
      `SELECT password_hash FROM "user" WHERE id = $1 AND is_active = true LIMIT 1`,
      [userId]
    );

    if (userResult.rowCount === 0) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "User not found" });
    }

    const { password_hash } = userResult.rows[0];

    // 2. Verify current password
    const { comparePassword, hashPassword } = await import("../security/password");
    const isCorrect = await comparePassword(current_password, password_hash);
    if (!isCorrect) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: "Current password is incorrect" });
    }

    // 3. Hash and update new password
    const newHash = await hashPassword(new_password);

    await pool.query(
      `UPDATE "user" SET password_hash = $1 WHERE id = $2`,
      [newHash, userId]
    );

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(500).json({ error: "Failed to change password" });
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\controllers\student-fee-record.controller.ts =====

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { overrideStudentInstallmentPlan } from "../services/student-installment-plan-override.service";
import { getOwnFeeRecord } from "../services/student-fee-record-read.service";
import { pool } from "../db/db";

export async function overrideInstallmentPlanController(
  req: Request<{ studentFeeRecordId: string }>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN]);

  try {
    const { studentFeeRecordId } = req.params;

    if (!studentFeeRecordId || typeof studentFeeRecordId !== "string") {
      return res.status(400).json({
        success: false,
        error: "studentFeeRecordId is required",
      });
    }

    const { installments } = req.body;

    if (!Array.isArray(installments) || installments.length === 0) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        success: false,
        error: "installments must be a non-empty array",
      });
    }

    await overrideStudentInstallmentPlan({
      studentFeeRecordId,
      installments,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
  } catch (err: any) {
    const status = err.statusCode ?? 400;
    return res.status(status).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}
export async function getFeeRecordByStudentController(
  req: Request<{ studentUserId: string }>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);

  try {
    const { studentUserId } = req.params;

    if (!studentUserId || typeof studentUserId !== "string") {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "studentUserId is required" });
    }

    const result = await pool.query(
      `SELECT sfr.id, sfr.total_payable, sfr.discount_amount, sfr.fee_status
       FROM student_fee_record sfr
       WHERE sfr.student_user_id = $1
         AND sfr.institute_id = $2
       ORDER BY sfr.created_at DESC
       LIMIT 1`,
      [studentUserId, context.institute_id]
    );

    if (result.rowCount === 0) {
      return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: "No fee record found for this student" });
    }

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: result.rows[0] });
  } catch (err: any) {
    const status = err.statusCode ?? 500;
    return res.status(status).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
  }
}

      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\controllers\study-material.controller.ts =====

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { denyStudentMutation } from "../auth/deny-student";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { uploadFileToR2 } from "../services/r2-storage.service";
import { createStudyMaterial } from "../services/study-material-create.service";
import { listStudyMaterials } from "../services/study-material-list.service";
import { createAnnouncement } from "../services/announcement-create.service";
import { pool } from "../db/db";

// POST /api/study-materials/upload
export async function uploadStudyMaterialController(
  req: Request,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT, ROLES.TEACHER]);
  denyStudentMutation(context);

  try {
    const file = (req as any).file as Express.Multer.File | undefined;

    if (!file) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "No file uploaded" });
    }

    const {
      linked_type,
      linked_id,
      class_batch_id,
      title,
      description,
    } = req.body;

    let resolvedLinkedType: "TEST" | "ANNOUNCEMENT";
    let resolvedLinkedId: string;

    if (linked_type === "TEST" && linked_id) {
      resolvedLinkedType = "TEST" as any;
      resolvedLinkedId = linked_id;
    } else {
      if (!class_batch_id) {
        return res.status(400).json({
          success: false,
          error: "class_batch_id is required when no test is linked",
        });
      }

      const announcement = await createAnnouncement({
        announcementType: "GENERAL",
        announcementTitle: (title as string | undefined)?.trim() || file.originalname,
        message:
          (description as string | undefined)?.trim() ||
          `Study material shared: ${file.originalname}`,
        classBatchId: class_batch_id,
        schoolAttribute: null,
        actingUserId: context.user_id,
        actingRole: context.role_id,
        actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
      });

      resolvedLinkedType = "ANNOUNCEMENT";
      resolvedLinkedId = announcement.id;
    }

    const { fileUrl } = await uploadFileToR2({
      instituteId: context.institute_id,
      category:    "study-materials",
      fileName:    file.originalname,
      fileBuffer:  file.buffer,
      mimeType:    file.mimetype,
    });

    const material = await createStudyMaterial({
      linkedType:        resolvedLinkedType,
      linkedId:          resolvedLinkedId,
      fileUrl,
      actingUserId:      context.user_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
    });

    return res.status(201).json({ success: true, data: material });
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("[upload-study-material] Error:", err?.message ?? err);
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message ?? "Upload failed" });
  }
}

// GET /api/study-materials
export async function listStudyMaterialsController(
  req: Request,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  try {
    const classBatchId = (req.query.class_batch_id as string) ?? undefined;
    const linkedTestId = (req.query.linked_test_id  as string) ?? undefined;

    const materials = await listStudyMaterials({
      actingUserId:      context.user_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
      actingRole:        context.role_id,
      classBatchId,
      linkedTestId,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: materials });
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("[list-study-materials] Error:", err?.message ?? err);
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message ?? "Failed to fetch materials" });
  }
}

// DELETE /api/study-materials/:materialId
export async function deleteStudyMaterialController(
  req: Request<{ materialId: string }>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT, ROLES.TEACHER]);
  denyStudentMutation(context);

  try {
    const { materialId } = req.params;

    // Verify ownership + institute scope
    const check = await pool.query(
      `SELECT sm.id, sm.file_url, sm.institute_id, sm.created_by
       FROM study_material sm
       WHERE sm.id = $1 AND sm.is_active = true
       LIMIT 1`,
      [materialId]
    );

    if (check.rowCount === 0) {
      return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: "Material not found" });
    }

    if (check.rows[0].institute_id !== context.institute_id) {
      return res.status(403).json({ success: false, error: "Access denied" });
    }

    // Teachers may only delete materials they personally uploaded
    if (context.role_id === ROLES.TEACHER && check.rows[0].created_by !== context.user_id) {
      return res.status(403).json({ success: false, error: "Teachers can only delete their own uploads" });
    }

    // Soft delete in DB
    await pool.query(
      `UPDATE study_material
       SET is_active = false, deactivated_by = $1, deactivated_at = NOW()
       WHERE id = $2`,
      [context.user_id, materialId]
    );

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("[delete-study-material] Error:", err?.message ?? err);
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message ?? "Delete failed" });
  }
}


// GET /api/study-materials/:materialId/download
export async function getStudyMaterialDownloadUrlController(
  req: Request<{ materialId: string }>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;
  const { materialId } = req.params;

  try {
    const check = await pool.query(
      `SELECT sm.id, sm.file_url, sm.institute_id, sm.created_by
       FROM study_material sm
       WHERE sm.id = $1 AND sm.is_active = true
       LIMIT 1`,
      [materialId]
    );

    if (check.rowCount === 0) {
      return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: "Material not found" });
    }

    if (check.rows[0].institute_id !== context.institute_id) {
      return res.status(403).json({ success: false, error: "Access denied" });
    }

    const fileUrl: string = check.rows[0].file_url;

    // Extract the object key from the public URL
    // URL format: https://<public-url>/<instituteId>/<category>/<uuid>.<ext>
    const publicBase = (process.env.R2_PUBLIC_URL ?? "").replace(/\/$/, "");
    const objectKey = fileUrl.replace(`${publicBase}/`, "");

    // Use the last segment of the key as the filename
    const fileName = objectKey.split("/").pop() ?? "download";

    const { getPresignedDownloadUrl } = await import("../services/r2-storage.service");
    const downloadUrl = await getPresignedDownloadUrl(objectKey, fileName);

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: { url: downloadUrl } });
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("[study-material-download] Error:", err?.message ?? err);
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: "Failed to generate download URL" });
  }
}

import { Request, Response } from "express";

  listSubjectCatalog,

} from "../services/subject-catalog.service";

// GET /api/subject-catalog

export async function listSubjectCatalogController(
  req: Request,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  try {
    const subjects = await listSubjectCatalog({
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: subjects });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
  }
