// POST /api/subject-catalog
// Only Admin, Management, Teacher can add subjects
export async function addSubjectToCatalogController(
  req: Request,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT, ROLES.TEACHER]);
  denyStudentMutation(context);

  const { subject } = req.body;

  if (!subject || typeof subject !== "string" || !subject.trim()) {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "subject is required" });
  }

  try {
    await addSubjectToCatalog({
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      subject: subject.trim(),
    });

    // Return the updated full list after adding
    const { listSubjectCatalog } = await import("../services/subject-catalog.service");
    const updated = await listSubjectCatalog({
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
    });

    return res.status(201).json({ success: true, data: updated });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\controllers\teacher-profile.controller.ts =====

// src/controllers/teacher-profile.controller.ts

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { pool } from "../db/db";

export async function getTeacherProfileController(
  req: Request<{ teacherId: string }>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;
  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);

  const { teacherId } = req.params;

  try {
    // 1. Basic profile
    const profileResult = await pool.query(
      `SELECT
         u.id,
         u.login_identifier,
         u.is_active,
         u.created_at,
         up.full_name,
         up.mobile,
         up.email,
         up.address,
         COALESCE(
           json_agg(
             json_build_object(
               'id',      cb.id,
               'name',    cb.name,
               'subject', tcb.subject,
               'academic_year_label', ay.label,
               'student_count', (
                 SELECT COUNT(*)::int FROM student s
                 WHERE s.class_batch_id = cb.id AND s.is_active = true
               )
             ) ORDER BY cb.name
           ) FILTER (WHERE cb.id IS NOT NULL),
           '[]'
         ) AS assigned_batches
       FROM "user" u
       JOIN user_profile up ON up.user_id = u.id
       JOIN teacher t ON t.user_id = u.id
       LEFT JOIN teacher_class_batch tcb ON tcb.teacher_user_id = u.id
       LEFT JOIN class_batch cb ON cb.id = tcb.class_batch_id AND cb.is_active = true
       LEFT JOIN academic_year ay ON ay.id = cb.academic_year_id
       WHERE u.id = $1
         AND u.institute_id = $2
         AND u.role_id = $3
       GROUP BY u.id, u.login_identifier, u.is_active, u.created_at,
                up.full_name, up.mobile, up.email, up.address`,
      [teacherId, context.institute_id, ROLES.TEACHER]
    );

    if (profileResult.rowCount === 0) {
      return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: "Teacher not found" });
    }

    // 2. Tests conducted (most recent 5 for profile page)
    const testsResult = await pool.query(
      `SELECT
         t.id,
         t.test_name,
         t.subject,
         t.test_date,
         t.total_marks,
         cb.name AS batch_name,
         EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM marks m WHERE m.test_id = t.id LIMIT 1) AS has_marks
       FROM test t
       JOIN class_batch cb ON cb.id = t.class_batch_id
       WHERE t.created_by = $1
         AND cb.institute_id = $2
       ORDER BY t.test_date DESC
       LIMIT 5`,
      [teacherId, context.institute_id]
    );

    // 3. Tests conducted total count
    const testCountResult = await pool.query(
      `SELECT COUNT(*)::int AS total
       FROM test t
       JOIN class_batch cb ON cb.id = t.class_batch_id
       WHERE t.created_by = $1
         AND cb.institute_id = $2`,
      [teacherId, context.institute_id]
    );

    return res.status(200).json({
      success: true,
      data: {
        ...profileResult.rows[0],
        tests_conducted: testsResult.rows,
        tests_total: testCountResult.rows[0]?.total ?? 0,
      },
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("[teacher-profile] Error:", err?.message ?? err);
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: "Failed to fetch teacher profile" });
  }
}

// GET /api/teachers/:teacherId/tests — all tests for view all
export async function getTeacherTestsController(
  req: Request<{ teacherId: string }>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;
  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);

  const { teacherId } = req.params;
  const limit  = Math.min(parseInt((req.query.limit  as string) ?? "20", 10), 100);
  const offset = Math.max(parseInt((req.query.offset as string) ?? "0",  10), 0);

  try {
    // Verify teacher belongs to this institute
    const teacherCheck = await pool.query(
      `SELECT u.id FROM "user" u
       JOIN teacher t ON t.user_id = u.id
       WHERE u.id = $1 AND u.institute_id = $2 LIMIT 1`,
      [teacherId, context.institute_id]
    );

    if (teacherCheck.rowCount === 0) {
      return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: "Teacher not found" });
    }

    const result = await pool.query(
      `SELECT
         t.id,
         t.test_name,
         t.subject,
         t.test_date,
         t.total_marks,
         cb.name AS batch_name,
         EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM marks m WHERE m.test_id = t.id LIMIT 1) AS has_marks,
         COUNT(*) OVER() AS total_count
       FROM test t
       JOIN class_batch cb ON cb.id = t.class_batch_id
       WHERE t.created_by = $1
         AND cb.institute_id = $2
       ORDER BY t.test_date DESC
       LIMIT $3 OFFSET $4`,
      [teacherId, context.institute_id, limit, offset]
    );

    const total = result.rows[0]?.total_count ?? 0;

    return res.status(200).json({
      success: true,
      data: result.rows.map(({ total_count: _, ...row }) => row),
      total: Number(total),
      limit,
      offset,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("[teacher-tests] Error:", err?.message ?? err);
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: "Failed to fetch teacher tests" });
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\controllers\teacher.controller.ts =====

// src/controllers/teacher.controller.ts

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { assignTeacher } from "../services/teacher-create.service";
import { pool } from "../db/db";

// POST /api/teachers — assign a user as teacher with batch(es)
export async function assignTeacherController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);

  const { teacher_user_id, batch_assignments } = req.body;

  if (!teacher_user_id || typeof teacher_user_id !== "string") {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "teacher_user_id is required" });
  }

  if (!Array.isArray(batch_assignments) || batch_assignments.length === 0) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "batch_assignments must be a non-empty array" });
  }

  const batchAssignments: { batchId: string; subject: string | null }[] =
    batch_assignments.map((b: any) => ({
      batchId: b.batch_id,
      subject: typeof b.subject === "string" && b.subject.trim() ? b.subject.trim() : null,
    }));

  try {
    await assignTeacher({
      teacherUserId:    teacher_user_id,
      batchAssignments,
      actingUserId:     context.user_id,
      actingRole:       context.role_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
    });

    return res.status(201).json({ success: true });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
  }
}

// GET /api/users/teachers — teacher-role users not yet assigned in teacher table
export async function listUnassignedTeacherUsersController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);

  try {
    // Return teacher-role users who still have at least one active batch
    // in the active academic year that they are NOT yet assigned to.
    // Once a teacher is assigned to every batch in the active year, they
    // no longer appear here — there is nothing left to assign them to.
    const result = await pool.query(
      `SELECT u.id, up.full_name, u.login_identifier
       FROM "user" u
       JOIN user_profile up ON up.user_id = u.id
       WHERE u.institute_id = $1
         AND u.role_id      = $2
         AND u.is_active    = true
         AND EXISTS (
           -- at least one active batch in the active year they don't have yet
           SELECT 1
           FROM class_batch cb
           WHERE cb.institute_id = $1
             AND cb.is_active    = true
             AND cb.academic_year_id = (
               SELECT id FROM academic_year
               WHERE institute_id = $1 AND is_active = true
               LIMIT 1
             )
             AND NOT EXISTS (
               SELECT 1 FROM teacher_class_batch tcb
               WHERE tcb.teacher_user_id = u.id
                 AND tcb.class_batch_id  = cb.id
             )
         )
       ORDER BY up.full_name ASC`,
      [context.institute_id, ROLES.TEACHER]
    );

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: result.rows });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
  }
}

// DELETE /api/teachers/:teacherId/batches/:batchId — remove a batch assignment
export async function unassignTeacherBatchController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);

  const { teacherId, batchId } = req.params as { teacherId: string; batchId: string };

  try {
    // Verify the teacher belongs to this institute
    const teacherCheck = await pool.query(
      `SELECT u.id FROM "user" u
       JOIN teacher t ON t.user_id = u.id
       WHERE u.id = $1 AND u.institute_id = $2
       LIMIT 1`,
      [teacherId, context.institute_id]
    );

    if (teacherCheck.rowCount === 0) {
      return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: "Teacher not found" });
    }

    // Verify the batch belongs to this institute
    const batchCheck = await pool.query(
      `SELECT id FROM class_batch WHERE id = $1 AND institute_id = $2 LIMIT 1`,
      [batchId, context.institute_id]
    );

    if (batchCheck.rowCount === 0) {
      return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: "Batch not found" });
    }

    await pool.query(
      `DELETE FROM teacher_class_batch
       WHERE teacher_user_id = $1 AND class_batch_id = $2`,
      [teacherId, batchId]
    );

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
  }
}

// GET /api/class-batches — active batches for this institute
// Optional: ?academic_year_id=<uuid> → scopes results to that year only
export async function listClassBatchesController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;

  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT, ROLES.TEACHER]);

  const academicYearId = (req.query.academic_year_id as string | undefined)?.trim() || null;

  if (academicYearId) {
    // Verify the requested academic year actually belongs to this institute
    try {
      const yearCheck = await pool.query(
        `SELECT id FROM academic_year WHERE id = $1 AND institute_id = $2 LIMIT 1`,
        [academicYearId, context.institute_id]
      );
      if (yearCheck.rowCount === 0) {
        return res.status(403).json({ success: false, error: "Academic year not found or access denied." });
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
    }
  }

  try {
    const result = academicYearId
      ? await pool.query(
          `SELECT id, name, academic_year_id
           FROM class_batch
           WHERE institute_id = $1 AND is_active = true AND academic_year_id = $2
           ORDER BY name ASC`,
          [context.institute_id, academicYearId]
        )
      : await pool.query(
          `SELECT id, name, academic_year_id
           FROM class_batch
           WHERE institute_id = $1 AND is_active = true
           ORDER BY name ASC`,
          [context.institute_id]
        );

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: result.rows });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
  }
}

// GET /api/class-batches/page-summary
// Returns active batch count + total student count scoped to the active academic year
export async function getBatchesPageSummaryController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;
  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT, ROLES.TEACHER]);

  try {
    const result = await pool.query(
      `SELECT
         COUNT(DISTINCT cb.id)::int                      AS active_batches,
         COUNT(s.user_id)::int                           AS total_students
       FROM class_batch cb
       LEFT JOIN student s
         ON s.class_batch_id = cb.id
         AND s.is_active = true
         AND s.enrollment_state = 'ACTIVE'
       WHERE cb.institute_id = $1
         AND cb.is_active = true
         AND cb.academic_year_id = (
           SELECT id FROM academic_year
           WHERE institute_id = $1 AND is_active = true
           LIMIT 1
         )`,
      [context.institute_id]
    );

    const row = result.rows[0] ?? { active_batches: 0, total_students: 0 };
    return res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: row });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
  }
}

// GET /api/class-batches/detailed
// Returns full batch list for the active academic year, with created_by, assigned teachers, student count
export async function listBatchesDetailedController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;
  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT, ROLES.TEACHER]);

  try {
    const batchesResult = await pool.query(
      `SELECT
         cb.id,
         cb.name,
         cb.created_at,
         ay.label                                        AS academic_year_label,
         COALESCE(up.full_name, u.login_identifier)      AS created_by,
         COUNT(s.user_id)::int                           AS student_count
       FROM class_batch cb
       JOIN academic_year ay
         ON ay.id = cb.academic_year_id
       LEFT JOIN "user" u  ON u.id  = cb.created_by
       LEFT JOIN user_profile up ON up.user_id = cb.created_by
       LEFT JOIN student s
         ON s.class_batch_id = cb.id
         AND s.is_active = true
         AND s.enrollment_state = 'ACTIVE'
       WHERE cb.institute_id = $1
         AND cb.is_active = true
         AND cb.academic_year_id = (
           SELECT id FROM academic_year
           WHERE institute_id = $1 AND is_active = true
           LIMIT 1
         )
       GROUP BY cb.id, cb.name, cb.created_at, ay.label, up.full_name, u.login_identifier
       ORDER BY cb.name ASC`,
      [context.institute_id]
    );

    if (batchesResult.rows.length === 0) {
      return res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: [] });
    }

    const batchIds: string[] = batchesResult.rows.map((r) => r.id);

    // Fetch all assigned teachers for these batches in one query
    const teachersResult = await pool.query(
      `SELECT
         tcb.class_batch_id,
         COALESCE(up.full_name, u.login_identifier) AS teacher_name
       FROM teacher_class_batch tcb
       JOIN "user" u  ON u.id  = tcb.teacher_user_id
       LEFT JOIN user_profile up ON up.user_id = tcb.teacher_user_id
       WHERE tcb.class_batch_id = ANY($1::uuid[])`,
      [batchIds]
    );

    // Group teachers by batch_id
    const teachersByBatch: Record<string, string[]> = {};
    for (const row of teachersResult.rows) {
      if (!teachersByBatch[row.class_batch_id]) teachersByBatch[row.class_batch_id] = [];
      teachersByBatch[row.class_batch_id].push(row.teacher_name);
    }

    const data = batchesResult.rows.map((b) => ({
      id:                  b.id,
      name:                b.name,
      created_at:          b.created_at,
      academic_year_label: b.academic_year_label,
      created_by:          b.created_by,
      student_count:       b.student_count,
      teachers:            teachersByBatch[b.id] ?? [],
    }));

    return res.status(200).json({ success: true, data });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
  }
}

// GET /api/class-batches/:batchId/students?limit=5&offset=0
// Returns students enrolled in a batch; institute-scoped for security
export async function getBatchStudentsController(
  req: Request<{ batchId: string }>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;
  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT, ROLES.TEACHER]);

  const { batchId } = req.params;
  const limit  = Math.min(parseInt((req.query.limit  as string) ?? "5",  10), 100);
  const offset = Math.max(parseInt((req.query.offset as string) ?? "0",  10), 0);

  try {
    // Verify batch belongs to this institute
    const batchCheck = await pool.query(
      `SELECT id FROM class_batch WHERE id = $1 AND institute_id = $2 AND is_active = true LIMIT 1`,
      [batchId, context.institute_id]
    );
    if (batchCheck.rowCount === 0) {
      return res.status(403).json({ success: false, error: "Batch not found or access denied." });
    }

    const countResult = await pool.query(
      `SELECT COUNT(*)::int AS total FROM student WHERE class_batch_id = $1 AND is_active = true AND enrollment_state = 'ACTIVE'`,
      [batchId]
    );
    const total: number = countResult.rows[0]?.total ?? 0;

    const studentsResult = await pool.query(
      `SELECT
         s.user_id                                        AS id,
         COALESCE(up.full_name, u.login_identifier)       AS name,
         u.login_identifier
       FROM student s
       JOIN "user" u         ON u.id         = s.user_id
       LEFT JOIN user_profile up ON up.user_id = s.user_id
       WHERE s.class_batch_id = $1
         AND s.is_active = true
         AND s.enrollment_state = 'ACTIVE'
       ORDER BY COALESCE(up.full_name, u.login_identifier) ASC
       LIMIT $2 OFFSET $3`,
      [batchId, limit, offset]
    );

    return res.status(200).json({
      success: true,
      data:  studentsResult.rows,
      total,
      limit,
      offset,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
  }
}

// POST /api/tests/:testId/marks/bulk
export async function bulkSubmitMarksController(
  req: Request<{ testId: string }>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;
  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT, ROLES.TEACHER]);

  const { entries, mode } = req.body as {
    entries: { student_id: string; score: number | null }[];
    mode: "enter" | "modify";
  };

  if (!Array.isArray(entries) || entries.length === 0) {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "entries array is required" });
  }
  if (mode !== "enter" && mode !== "modify") {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "mode must be 'enter' or 'modify'" });
  }

  try {
    await bulkSubmitMarks({
      testId: req.params.testId,
      entries,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
      mode,
    });
    return res.status(200).json({ success: true });
  } catch (err: any) {
    const status =
      err.message.includes("denied") ? 403 :
      err.message.includes("not found") ? 404 :
      err.message.includes("already exist") ? 409 : 400;
    return res.status(status).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
  }
}


// ===== FILE: src\controllers\test.controller.ts =====

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { createTest } from "../services/test-create.service";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { denyStudentMutation } from "../auth/deny-student";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { updateTest } from "../services/test-update.service";
import { deleteTest } from "../services/test-delete.service";
import { getTestRanking } from "../services/test-ranking.service";
import { getStudentPublishedMarks } from "../services/student-test-view.service";




export async function createTestController(
  req: Request,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  // 🔐 Role enforcement (MA-016)
  requireRole(context, [
    ROLES.ADMIN,
    ROLES.MANAGEMENT,
    ROLES.TEACHER,
  ]);

  // 🚫 Absolute student mutation block
  denyStudentMutation(context);

  try {
    const {
      class_batch_ids,
      test_name,
      subject,
      syllabus_text,
      test_date,
      test_time,
      duration_minutes,
      total_marks,
      is_canonical_subject,
    } = req.body;

    if (!test_name?.trim()) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "test_name is required" });
    }
    if (!subject?.trim()) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "subject is required" });
    }
    if (!test_date) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "test_date is required" });
    }
    if (!total_marks || Number(total_marks) <= 0) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "total_marks must be greater than 0" });
    }
    if (!Array.isArray(class_batch_ids) || class_batch_ids.length === 0) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "class_batch_ids must be a non-empty array" });
    }

    // One test row + one announcement per batch — sequential, all-or-nothing feel
    // (if one fails mid-way the ones before are committed; acceptable for v1)
    const results = [];
    for (const batchId of class_batch_ids as string[]) {
      const test = await createTest({
        classBatchId: batchId,
        testName: String(test_name).trim(),
        subject: String(subject).trim(),
        syllabusText: syllabus_text ?? null,
        testDate: String(test_date),
        testTime: test_time ?? null,
        durationMinutes: duration_minutes != null ? Number(duration_minutes) : null,
        totalMarks: Number(total_marks),
        isCanonicalSubject: is_canonical_subject ?? true,
        actingUserId: context.user_id,
        actingRole: context.role_id,
        actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
      });
      results.push(test);
    }

    return res.status(201).json({
      success: true,
      created: results.length,
      data: results,
    });

  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}


type UpdateTestParams = {
  testId: string;
};

export async function updateTestController(
  req: Request<UpdateTestParams>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;

  // 🔐 Role enforcement (MA-017)
  requireRole(context, [
    ROLES.ADMIN,
    ROLES.MANAGEMENT,
    ROLES.TEACHER,
  ]);

  // 🚫 Students cannot mutate
  denyStudentMutation(context);

  try {
    const { testId } = req.params;

    const {
      subject,
      syllabus_text,
      test_date,
      test_time,
      duration_minutes,
    } = req.body;

    const updated = await updateTest({
      testId,
      subject,
      syllabusText: syllabus_text,
      testDate: test_date,
      testTime: test_time !== undefined ? (test_time ?? null) : undefined,
      durationMinutes: duration_minutes !== undefined ? (duration_minutes != null ? Number(duration_minutes) : null) : undefined,
      actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
      actingUserId: context.user_id,
      actingRole: context.role_id,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({
      success: true,
      data: updated,
    });

  } catch (err: any) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      success: false,
      error: err.message,
    });
  }
}

import { getBatchStudents } from "../services/batch-students.service";

// GET /api/tests/:testId/students
export async function getTestBatchStudentsController(
  req: Request<{ testId: string }>,
  res: Response
) {
  const context = req.context!;
  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT, ROLES.TEACHER]);

  try {
    // Resolve batch from test, enforce institute scope
    const testResult = await (await import("../db/db")).pool.query(
      `SELECT t.class_batch_id, cb.institute_id
       FROM test t
       JOIN class_batch cb ON cb.id = t.class_batch_id
       WHERE t.id = $1 LIMIT 1`,
      [req.params.testId]
    );
    if (testResult.rowCount === 0) return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: "Test not found" });
    const { class_batch_id, institute_id } = testResult.rows[0];
    if (institute_id !== context.institute_id) return res.status(403).json({ success: false, error: "Access denied" });

    const students = await getBatchStudents(class_batch_id, context.institute_id);
    return res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: students });
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("[test-batch-students] Error:", err?.message ?? err);
    return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: "Failed to fetch batch students" });
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\controllers\user.controller.ts =====

import { Request, Response } from "express";
import { generateLoginIdentifier } from "../auth/login-identifier.service";
import { deactivateUser } from "../services/user-deactivation.service";
import { requireRole } from "../auth/require-role";
import { ROLES } from "../auth/roles";
import { ForbiddenError } from "../auth/auth.errors";
import { dispatchNotification } from "../notifications/notification-dispatch.service";
import { autoCreateStudentFeeRecord } from "../services/student-fee-record-create.service";
import { pool } from "../db/db";
import { hashPassword } from "../security/password";
import { randomUUID } from "crypto";

export async function createUserController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;
  const roleId = req.body.role;
  const fullName: string | undefined = req.body.full_name?.trim();
  const instituteId = req.inheritedInstituteId!;

  if (!fullName) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "full_name is required" });
  }

  const userId = randomUUID();
  const loginIdentifier = generateLoginIdentifier(roleId);

  const temporaryPassword = randomUUID().split("-")[0]!;
  const passwordHash = await hashPassword(temporaryPassword);

  // Student-specific fields — only required when role is STUDENT
  const fatherName: string | undefined        = req.body.father_name?.trim();
  const mobile: string | undefined            = req.body.mobile?.trim();
  const alternateMobile: string | undefined   = req.body.alternate_mobile?.trim();
  const schoolName: string | undefined        = req.body.school_name?.trim();
  const educationBoard: string | undefined    = req.body.education_board?.trim();
  const classBatchId: string | undefined      = req.body.class_batch_id?.trim() || undefined;
  const academicYearId: string | undefined    = req.body.academic_year_id?.trim();
  const email: string | undefined             = req.body.email?.trim().toLowerCase();
  const address: string | undefined           = req.body.address?.trim();
  const discountAmount: number | undefined    = req.body.discount_amount != null
                                                  ? Number(req.body.discount_amount)
                                                  : undefined;
  const discountReason: string | undefined    = req.body.discount_reason?.trim() || undefined;

  // Email format validation if provided
  if (email && !/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(email)) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "Invalid email format" });
  }

  // Mobile format validation if provided (10-digit Indian mobile)
  if (mobile && !/^\d{10}$/.test(mobile)) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "Mobile must be a 10-digit number" });
  }

  if (roleId === ROLES.STUDENT) {
    if (!mobile) return res.status(400).json({ error: "mobile is required for students" });
    if (!schoolName) return res.status(400).json({ error: "school_name is required for students" });
    if (!educationBoard) return res.status(400).json({ error: "education_board is required for students" });
    if (!academicYearId) return res.status(400).json({ error: "academic_year_id is required for students" });
  }

  // Discount field validation — Teachers and Students cannot supply discount fields
  if (discountAmount !== undefined || discountReason !== undefined) {
    if (roleId !== ROLES.STUDENT) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        error: "Discount fields are only applicable when enrolling a student",
      });
    }
    if (
      context.role_id !== ROLES.ADMIN &&
      context.role_id !== ROLES.MANAGEMENT
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({
        error: "Only Admin or Management can apply discounts",
      });
    }
    if (discountAmount !== undefined) {
      if (isNaN(discountAmount) || discountAmount < 0) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: "discount_amount must be a non-negative number" });
      }
      if (discountAmount > 0 && !discountReason) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: "discount_reason is required when discount_amount is greater than 0" });
      }
    }
  }

  if (roleId === ROLES.TEACHER || roleId === ROLES.MANAGEMENT) {
    if (!mobile) return res.status(400).json({ error: "mobile is required for teachers and management" });
    if (!email) return res.status(400).json({ error: "email is required for teachers and management" });
  }

  const client = await pool.connect();
  try {
    await client.query("BEGIN");

    const result = await client.query(
      `INSERT INTO "user" (
        id, institute_id, role_id, login_identifier,
        password_hash, is_active, created_at, created_by
      )
      VALUES ($1,$2,$3,$4,$5,true,NOW(),$6)
      RETURNING id, login_identifier, institute_id, role_id`,
      [userId, instituteId, roleId, loginIdentifier, passwordHash, context.user_id]
    );

    await client.query(
      `INSERT INTO user_profile (
        user_id, full_name, father_name, mobile, alternate_mobile,
        school_name, education_board, email, address, created_at
      )
      VALUES ($1,$2,$3,$4,$5,$6,$7,$8,$9,NOW())`,
      [
        userId,
        fullName,
        fatherName ?? null,
        mobile ?? null,
        alternateMobile ?? null,
        schoolName ?? null,
        educationBoard ?? null,
        email ?? null,
        address ?? null,
      ]
    );

    // Insert student row only when role is STUDENT
    if (roleId === ROLES.STUDENT) {
      // Verify academic year belongs to institute
      const yearCheck = await client.query(
        `SELECT id FROM academic_year WHERE id = $1 AND institute_id = $2 LIMIT 1`,
        [academicYearId, instituteId]
      );
      if (yearCheck.rowCount === 0) {
        throw new Error("Academic year not found or does not belong to this institute");
      }

      // Verify batch belongs to institute (if provided)
      if (classBatchId) {
        const batchCheck = await client.query(
          `SELECT id FROM class_batch WHERE id = $1 AND institute_id = $2 AND is_active = true LIMIT 1`,
          [classBatchId, instituteId]
        );
        if (batchCheck.rowCount === 0) {
          throw new Error("Batch not found or does not belong to this institute");
        }
      }

      await client.query(
        `INSERT INTO student (
          user_id, academic_year_id, class_batch_id,
          is_active, created_at, created_by
        )
        VALUES ($1,$2,$3,true,NOW(),$4)`,
        [userId, academicYearId, classBatchId ?? null, context.user_id]
      );

      // Auto-create fee record if the batch has an active fee structure.
      // Non-blocking: if no fee structure exists enrollment still succeeds.
      // Only attempt when a class_batch_id was actually provided.
      if (classBatchId) {
        await autoCreateStudentFeeRecord({
          studentUserId: userId,
          classBatchId,
          instituteId,
          actingUserId: context.user_id,
          discountAmount: discountAmount ?? 0,
          discountReason: discountReason ?? null,
          client,
        });
      }
    }

    await client.query("COMMIT");

    // 🔔 Emit notifications after successful commit
    if (roleId === ROLES.STUDENT) {
      // 1. Welcome notification → student only
      await dispatchNotification({
        type: "STUDENT_ACCOUNT_CREATED",
        entityId: userId,
        instituteId: instituteId,
        metadata: {
          studentUserId: userId,
          loginIdentifier: loginIdentifier,
        },
      });

      // 2. Enrollment summary → Admin + Management only
      // Resolve batch name and fee total for the message
      let batchName: string | null = null;
      let totalPayable: number | null = null;

      if (classBatchId) {
        const batchRow = await pool.query(
          `SELECT name FROM class_batch WHERE id = $1 LIMIT 1`,
          [classBatchId]
        );
        batchName = batchRow.rows[0]?.name ?? null;

        const feeRow = await pool.query(
          `SELECT total_payable FROM student_fee_record
           WHERE student_user_id = $1 AND institute_id = $2
           ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT 1`,
          [userId, instituteId]
        );
        totalPayable = feeRow.rows[0]?.total_payable != null
          ? Number(feeRow.rows[0].total_payable)
          : null;
      }

      await dispatchNotification({
        type: "STUDENT_ENROLLED",
        entityId: userId,
        instituteId: instituteId,
        metadata: {
          studentName: fullName,
          batchName: batchName,
          totalPayable: totalPayable,
        },
      });
    }

    return res.status(201).json({
      message: "User provisioned successfully",
      user: result.rows[0],
      temporary_password: temporaryPassword, // v1 only
    });

  } catch (err: any) {
    await client.query("ROLLBACK");
    return res.status(500).json({ error: err.message ?? "User creation failed" });
  } finally {
    client.release();
  }
}
export async function deactivateUserController(req: Request, res: Response) {
  const context = req.context!;
  const rawUserId = req.params.userId;

if (!rawUserId || typeof rawUserId !== "string") {
  return res.status(400).json({
    error: "Invalid or missing userId parameter",
  });
}

const targetUserId = rawUserId;

  // Only Admin & Management allowed (MA-05)
  requireRole(context, [ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.MANAGEMENT]);

  await deactivateUser({
    targetUserId,
    actingUserId: context.user_id,
    actingInstituteId: context.institute_id,
  });

  return res.status(200).json({
    message: "User deactivated successfully",
  });
}

  database: process.env.DB_NAME,

  },
});

import 'dotenv/config';

// ===== FILE: src\jobs\job-runner.ts =====

import { runOverdueSweep } from "./overdue-sweep.job";

/**
 * Lightweight in-process job scheduler.
 *
 * Runs jobs on a fixed interval using setInterval.
 * This is sufficient for v1 — no external queue or pg_cron dependency needed.
 *
 * Jobs run immediately on server start (to catch any overnight drift),
 * then on their configured interval thereafter.
 *
 * All jobs are fire-and-forget with internal error handling —
 * a failing job never crashes the server process.
 */

const OVERDUE_SWEEP_INTERVAL_MS = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 24 hours

function safeRun(name: string, fn: () => Promise<void>): void {
  fn().catch((err) => {
    console.error(`[job-runner] Unhandled error in job "${name}":`, err);
  });
}

export function startJobRunner(): void {
  console.log("[job-runner] Starting scheduled jobs...");

  // Run immediately on boot to catch any overnight drift
  safeRun("overdue-sweep", runOverdueSweep);

  // Then run every 24 hours
  setInterval(() => {
    safeRun("overdue-sweep", runOverdueSweep);
  }, OVERDUE_SWEEP_INTERVAL_MS);

  console.log(
    `[job-runner] overdue-sweep scheduled every ${OVERDUE_SWEEP_INTERVAL_MS / 3600000}h`
  );
}

// ===== FILE: src\jobs\overdue-sweep.job.ts =====

import { pool } from "../db/db";
import { recomputeFeeStatus } from "../services/fee-status-recompute.service";

/**
 * Nightly OVERDUE sweep job.
 *
 * Finds all student_fee_records that are not yet PAID and triggers
 * recomputeFeeStatus on each one. This is the only way OVERDUE status
 * can be set for students who have had no recent payment activity.
 *
 * Event-driven recomputation (payment insert / cancel) handles the real-time
 * case. This job handles the time-passage case — a student whose installment
 * due_date has passed since their last payment event.
 *
 * Safe to run multiple times — recomputeFeeStatus is idempotent.
 * Uses a dedicated system actor ID for the updated_by audit trail.
 */

// null is used as the system actor for automated jobs —
// updated_by FK allows NULL per schema definition
const SYSTEM_ACTOR_ID = null;

export async function runOverdueSweep(): Promise<void> {
  console.log("[overdue-sweep] Starting sweep...");

  // 1️⃣ Fetch all non-PAID fee records across all institutes
  // We exclude PAID because they have no outstanding balance —
  // recomputeFeeStatus would confirm PAID and do a redundant write.
  const recordsResult = await pool.query<{ id: string; institute_id: string }>(
    `SELECT id, institute_id
     FROM student_fee_record
     WHERE fee_status != 'PAID'
     ORDER BY institute_id ASC, id ASC`
  );

  const records = recordsResult.rows;
  console.log(`[overdue-sweep] Found ${records.length} non-PAID records to check.`);

  let updated = 0;
  let errors = 0;

  // 2️⃣ Recompute each record — standalone (no transaction client passed)
  // Each recompute is independent; a failure on one record must not
  // block the rest of the sweep.
  for (const record of records) {
    try {
      const { newFeeStatus } = await recomputeFeeStatus(
        record.id,
        SYSTEM_ACTOR_ID
      );

      if (newFeeStatus === "OVERDUE") {
        updated++;
        console.log(
          `[overdue-sweep] Marked OVERDUE: fee_record=${record.id} institute=${record.institute_id}`
        );
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      errors++;
      console.error(
        `[overdue-sweep] Failed for fee_record=${record.id}: ${err?.message ?? err}`
      );
    }
  }

  console.log(
    `[overdue-sweep] Complete. overdue_marked=${updated} errors=${errors} total_checked=${records.length}`
  );
}

// ===== FILE: src\middleware\upload.middleware.ts =====

import multer from "multer";

const MAX_FILE_SIZE_MB = 50;

export const uploadMiddleware = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: {
    fileSize: MAX_FILE_SIZE_MB * 1024 * 1024,
  },
  fileFilter: (_req, file, cb) => {
    const ALLOWED_MIME_TYPES = [
      "application/pdf",
      "image/jpeg",
      "image/png",
      "image/gif",
      "image/webp",
      "video/mp4",
      "video/quicktime",
      "video/x-msvideo",
      "application/msword",
      "application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document",
      "application/vnd.ms-powerpoint",
      "application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.presentationml.presentation",
      "text/plain",
    ];

    if (ALLOWED_MIME_TYPES.includes(file.mimetype)) {
      cb(null, true);
    } else {
      cb(new Error(`File type ${file.mimetype} is not allowed`));
    }
  },
});

// ===== FILE: src\Modules\Attendance\attendance-create.service.ts =====

import { pool } from "../../db/db";
import { randomUUID } from "crypto";
import { dispatchNotification } from "../../notifications/notification-dispatch.service";
import { isHoliday } from "../../services/holiday-check.service";

type CreateAttendanceInput = {
  studentId: string;
  classBatchId: string;
  attendanceDate: string; // ISO date string
  status: string; // ENUM enforced by DB
  late: boolean;
  earlyLeave: boolean;
  markedBy: string;
  actingInstituteId: string;
};

export async function createAttendanceRecord(
  input: CreateAttendanceInput
) {
  const studentQuery = `
    SELECT
      s.user_id,
      s.class_batch_id,
      u.institute_id AS "instituteId"
    FROM student s
    JOIN "user" u ON u.id = s.user_id
    WHERE s.user_id = $1
    LIMIT 1
  `;

  const studentResult = await pool.query(studentQuery, [
    input.studentId,
  ]);

  if (studentResult.rowCount === 0) {
    throw new Error("Student not found");
  }

  const student = studentResult.rows[0];

  if (student.instituteId !== input.actingInstituteId) {
    throw new Error("Cross-institute attendance creation denied");
  }

  if (student.class_batch_id !== input.classBatchId) {
    throw new Error(
      "Student does not belong to provided class batch"
    );
  }

  const holiday = await isHoliday({
    instituteId: input.actingInstituteId,
    date: input.attendanceDate,
    classBatchId: input.classBatchId,
  });

  if (holiday) {
    throw new Error("Attendance cannot be marked on a declared holiday");
  }

  const enrollmentCheck = await pool.query(
    `SELECT created_at::date AS enrolled_on
     FROM student
     WHERE user_id = $1
     LIMIT 1`,
    [input.studentId]
  );

  if (enrollmentCheck.rowCount! > 0) {
    const enrolledOn: string = enrollmentCheck.rows[0].enrolled_on;
    if (input.attendanceDate < enrolledOn) {
      throw new Error(
        `Student was not enrolled on ${input.attendanceDate} (enrolled ${enrolledOn})`
      );
    }
  }

  const insertQuery = `
    INSERT INTO attendance_record (
      id,
      student_id,
      class_batch_id,
      attendance_date,
      status,
      late,
      early_leave,
      marked_by,
      created_by,
      updated_by
    )
    VALUES ($1,$2,$3,$4,$5,$6,$7,$8,$8,$8)
    RETURNING *
  `;

  const attendanceId = randomUUID();

  const insertResult = await pool.query(insertQuery, [
    attendanceId,
    input.studentId,
    input.classBatchId,
    input.attendanceDate,
    input.status,
    input.late,
    input.earlyLeave,
    input.markedBy,
  ]);

  const createdRecord = insertResult.rows[0];

  if (input.status === "absent") {
    await dispatchNotification({
      type: "STUDENT_ABSENT",
      entityId: attendanceId,
      instituteId: input.actingInstituteId,
      metadata: {
        studentId: input.studentId,
        date: input.attendanceDate,
      },
    });
  }

  if (input.late === true) {
    await dispatchNotification({
      type: "STUDENT_LATE",
      entityId: attendanceId,
      instituteId: input.actingInstituteId,
      metadata: {
        studentId: input.studentId,
        date: input.attendanceDate,
      },
    });
  }

  if (input.earlyLeave === true) {
    await dispatchNotification({
      type: "STUDENT_EARLY_LEAVE",
      entityId: attendanceId,
      instituteId: input.actingInstituteId,
      metadata: {
        studentId: input.studentId,
        date: input.attendanceDate,
      },
    });
  }

  return createdRecord;
}


// ===== FILE: src\notifications\notification-dedup.service.ts =====

// ============================================
// DOMAIN 3.5.7
// Notification Dedup / Replacement Utility
// ============================================

import { pool } from "../db/db";
import { randomUUID } from "crypto";

type InsertNotificationInput = {
  type: string;
  entityId: string;
  instituteId: string;
  recipientUserId: string;
  message: string;
  replaceExisting?: boolean;
};

/**
 * Centralized insert logic for notifications.
 * Handles:
 *  - dedup_key generation
 *  - silent duplicate skip
 *  - replacement (mark obsolete before insert)
 */
export async function insertNotificationWithDedup(
  input: InsertNotificationInput
): Promise<void> {
  const {
    type,
    entityId,
    instituteId,
    recipientUserId,
    message,
    replaceExisting = false,
  } = input;

  const dedupKey = `${type}:${entityId}:${recipientUserId}`;

  // 🔁 Replacement logic
  if (replaceExisting) {
    await pool.query(
      `
      UPDATE notification
      SET is_obsolete = true
      WHERE dedup_key LIKE $1
        AND institute_id = $2
        AND is_obsolete = false
      `,
      [`${type}:${entityId}:%`, instituteId]
    );
  }

  try {
    await pool.query(
      `
      INSERT INTO notification (
        id,
        institute_id,
        event_type,
        entity_id,
        recipient_user_id,
        message,
        dedup_key,
        created_at
      )
      VALUES ($1,$2,$3,$4,$5,$6,$7,NOW())
      `,
      [
        randomUUID(),
        instituteId,
        type,
        entityId,
        recipientUserId,
        message,
        dedupKey,
      ]
    );

  } catch (err: any) {
    // 23505 = UNIQUE violation (dedup_key)
    if (err.code === "23505") {
      return; // silently skip
    }

    throw err;
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\notifications\notification-dispatch.service.ts =====

// ============================================
// DOMAIN 3.5.1.d
// Notification Dispatch Service
// ============================================

import { pool } from "../db/db";
import { EmitNotificationEventInput } from "./notification-event.types";
import { insertNotificationWithDedup } from "./notification-dedup.service";

/**
 * Central entry point for all notification events.
 * Business services must call this — never insert directly.
 *
 * Each event type has:
 *   - a fixed recipient rule (who receives it)
 *   - a message builder (what it says, using metadata for context)
 *
 * Admin/Management are NEVER recipients of per-student attendance events —
 * that would flood their panel. They receive aggregate/operational events only.
 */
export async function dispatchNotification(
  input: EmitNotificationEventInput
): Promise<void> {
  const { type, entityId, instituteId, metadata } = input;

  const recipients = await resolveRecipients({ type, entityId, instituteId, metadata });
  if (recipients.length === 0) return;

  const messagePerRecipient = buildMessages(type, metadata ?? {});

  for (const { userId, message } of recipients) {
    const resolvedMessage = message ?? messagePerRecipient.default;
    await insertNotificationWithDedup({
      type,
      entityId,
      instituteId,
      recipientUserId: userId,
      message: resolvedMessage,
      replaceExisting: metadata?.replaceExisting === true,
    });
  }
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// RECIPIENT RESOLUTION
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

type ResolvedRecipient = { userId: string; message?: string };

async function resolveRecipients(params: {
  type: string;
  entityId: string;
  instituteId: string;
  metadata?: Record<string, any>;
}): Promise<ResolvedRecipient[]> {
  const { type, instituteId, metadata } = params;

  // ── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  async function getAdminsAndManagement(): Promise<string[]> {
    const r = await pool.query(
      `SELECT id FROM "user"
       WHERE institute_id = $1 AND is_active = true AND role_id IN (1, 2)`,
      [instituteId]
    );
    return r.rows.map((row: any) => row.id);
  }

  async function getBatchStudents(classBatchId: string): Promise<string[]> {
    const r = await pool.query(
      `SELECT s.user_id
       FROM student s
       JOIN "user" u ON u.id = s.user_id
       WHERE s.class_batch_id = $1
         AND s.is_active = true
         AND u.institute_id = $2
         AND u.is_active = true`,
      [classBatchId, instituteId]
    );
    return r.rows.map((row: any) => row.user_id);
  }

  async function getBatchTeachers(classBatchId: string): Promise<string[]> {
    const r = await pool.query(
      `SELECT tcb.teacher_user_id
       FROM teacher_class_batch tcb
       JOIN "user" u ON u.id = tcb.teacher_user_id
       WHERE tcb.class_batch_id = $1
         AND u.institute_id = $2
         AND u.is_active = true`,
      [classBatchId, instituteId]
    );
    return r.rows.map((row: any) => row.teacher_user_id);
  }

  async function getAllInstituteUsers(): Promise<string[]> {
    const r = await pool.query(
      `SELECT id FROM "user" WHERE institute_id = $1 AND is_active = true`,
      [instituteId]
    );
    return r.rows.map((row: any) => row.id);
  }

  function unique(ids: string[]): ResolvedRecipient[] {
    return [...new Set(ids)].map((id) => ({ userId: id }));
  }

  // ── Per-event recipient logic ─────────────────────────────────────────────

  switch (type) {

    // Student receives their own attendance notification only.
    // Admin/Management do NOT get individual absent pings — too noisy.
    case "STUDENT_ABSENT":
    case "STUDENT_LATE":
    case "STUDENT_EARLY_LEAVE": {
      if (!metadata?.studentId) return [];
      return [{ userId: metadata.studentId }];
    }

    // Student gets welcome notification with their login ID.
    case "STUDENT_ACCOUNT_CREATED": {
      if (!metadata?.studentUserId) return [];
      return [{ userId: metadata.studentUserId }];
    }

    // Admin + Management get a single enrollment summary notification.
    case "STUDENT_ENROLLED": {
      const staff = await getAdminsAndManagement();
      return unique(staff);
    }

    // Test scheduled → batch students + batch teachers
    case "TEST_CREATED":
    case "TEST_DATE_UPDATED": {
      const classBatchId = metadata?.classBatchId;
      if (!classBatchId) return [];
      const [students, teachers] = await Promise.all([
        getBatchStudents(classBatchId),
        getBatchTeachers(classBatchId),
      ]);
      return unique([...students, ...teachers]);
    }

    // Results → batch students only (teachers already know, admin doesn't need it)
    case "TEST_RESULT_PUBLISHED": {
      const classBatchId = metadata?.classBatchId;
      if (!classBatchId) return [];
      const students = await getBatchStudents(classBatchId);
      return unique(students);
    }

    // Announcements — batch-scoped or institute-wide
    case "HOLIDAY_DECLARED":
    case "GENERAL_ANNOUNCEMENT":
    case "TEST_DAY_ANNOUNCED":
    case "PARENT_TEACHER_MEETING": {
      const classBatchId = metadata?.classBatchId ?? null;
      if (classBatchId) {
        const [students, teachers] = await Promise.all([
          getBatchStudents(classBatchId),
          getBatchTeachers(classBatchId),
        ]);
        return unique([...students, ...teachers]);
      }
      // Institute-wide: everyone
      const all = await getAllInstituteUsers();
      return unique(all);
    }

    // Study material — resolve batch from linked entity, then batch members
    case "STUDY_MATERIAL_UPLOADED": {
      const { linkedType, linkedId } = metadata ?? {};
      if (!linkedType || !linkedId) return [];

      const table = linkedType === "TEST" ? "test" : "announcement";
      const entityResult = await pool.query(
        `SELECT class_batch_id FROM ${table} WHERE id = $1 LIMIT 1`,
        [linkedId]
      );
      if ((entityResult.rowCount ?? 0) === 0) return [];

      const classBatchId: string | null = entityResult.rows[0].class_batch_id;
      if (!classBatchId) return [];

      const [students, teachers] = await Promise.all([
        getBatchStudents(classBatchId),
        getBatchTeachers(classBatchId),
      ]);
      return unique([...students, ...teachers]);
    }

    // Fee payment — student gets their own receipt summary;
    // Admin + Management get a collection summary (different message via metadata flag)
    case "FEE_PAYMENT_RECEIVED": {
      const studentUserId = metadata?.studentUserId;
      if (!studentUserId) return [];

      const staff = await getAdminsAndManagement();
      const recipients: ResolvedRecipient[] = [];

      // Student message is personal
      recipients.push({
        userId: studentUserId,
        message: metadata?.messageForStudent ?? undefined,
      });

      // Staff message is operational
      for (const staffId of staff) {
        if (staffId !== studentUserId) {
          recipients.push({
            userId: staffId,
            message: metadata?.messageForStaff ?? undefined,
          });
        }
      }

      return recipients;
    }

    default:
      return [];
  }
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// MESSAGE BUILDERS
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

/**
 * Builds human-readable notification messages from event type + metadata.
 * Returns { default } used when no per-recipient override is set.
 * Keep messages under ~100 chars — they are notifications, not essays.
 */
function buildMessages(
  type: string,
  meta: Record<string, any>
): { default: string } {
  const fmt = (d: string | undefined) => {
    if (!d) return "today";
    return new Date(d).toLocaleDateString("en-IN", {
      day: "numeric",
      month: "short",
    });
  };

  switch (type) {
    case "STUDENT_ABSENT":
      return {
        default: `You were marked absent on ${fmt(meta.date)}. Contact your teacher if this is a mistake.`,
      };

    case "STUDENT_LATE":
      return {
        default: `Late arrival noted for ${fmt(meta.date)}. Try to be on time for the next session.`,
      };

    case "STUDENT_EARLY_LEAVE":
      return {
        default: `Early leave recorded for ${fmt(meta.date)}. Hope everything's fine.`,
      };

    case "STUDENT_ACCOUNT_CREATED": {
      const loginId = meta.loginIdentifier ? ` Login ID: ${meta.loginIdentifier}.` : "";
      return {
        default: `Welcome to CleanDesk! Your student account is ready.${loginId}`,
      };
    }

    case "STUDENT_ENROLLED": {
      const name = meta.studentName ?? "A new student";
      const batch = meta.batchName ? ` in ${meta.batchName}` : "";
      const fees = meta.totalPayable != null
        ? ` Fees agreed: ₹${Number(meta.totalPayable).toLocaleString("en-IN")}.`
        : "";
      return {
        default: `${name} enrolled${batch}.${fees}`,
      };
    }

    case "TEST_CREATED": {
      const subject = meta.subject ?? "A";
      const name = meta.testName ?? "new test";
      const date = meta.testDate ? ` on ${fmt(meta.testDate)}` : "";
      const marks = meta.totalMarks ? ` (${meta.totalMarks} marks)` : "";
      return {
        default: `${subject} test scheduled — ${name}${marks}${date}. Start preparing!`,
      };
    }

    case "TEST_DATE_UPDATED": {
      const name = meta.testName ?? "A test";
      const date = meta.testDate ? ` to ${fmt(meta.testDate)}` : "";
      return {
        default: `Test rescheduled — ${name} moved${date}. Check your schedule.`,
      };
    }

    case "TEST_RESULT_PUBLISHED": {
      const subject = meta.subject ?? "Test";
      const name = meta.testName ?? "results";
      return {
        default: `Results out! ${subject} — ${name} results are declared. Check your score.`,
      };
    }

    case "HOLIDAY_DECLARED": {
      const holidayName = meta.holidayName ?? "a holiday";
      const date = meta.holidayDate ? ` on ${fmt(meta.holidayDate)}` : "";
      const scope = meta.batchName ? ` for ${meta.batchName}` : "";
      return {
        default: `Holiday announced: ${holidayName}${date}${scope}. No classes scheduled.`,
      };
    }

    case "GENERAL_ANNOUNCEMENT": {
      const title = meta.title ?? "New announcement";
      return {
        default: `${title} — check the Announcements section for details.`,
      };
    }

    case "TEST_DAY_ANNOUNCED": {
      const title = meta.title ?? "Test day scheduled";
      return {
        default: `${title} — check the Announcements section.`,
      };
    }

    case "PARENT_TEACHER_MEETING": {
      const title = meta.title ?? "Parent-Teacher Meeting scheduled";
      return {
        default: `${title} — check the Announcements section for time and details.`,
      };
    }

    case "STUDY_MATERIAL_UPLOADED": {
      const subject = meta.subject ?? "New material";
      const testName = meta.testName ?? null;
      const context = testName ? ` for ${testName}` : "";
      return {
        default: `New material added${subject !== "New material" ? ` — ${subject}` : ""}${context}. Check Study Materials.`,
      };
    }

    case "FEE_PAYMENT_RECEIVED":
      // Per-recipient messages are passed in metadata by the caller.
      // This default is a fallback only.
      return {
        default: meta.messageForStudent ?? "A fee payment has been recorded on your account.",
      };

    default:
      return { default: `New update: ${type.toLowerCase().replace(/_/g, " ")}.` };
  }
}

// ===== FILE: src\notifications\notification-event.types.ts =====

// ============================================
// DOMAIN 3.5.1.c
// Emit Notification Event Contract
// ============================================

export type EmitNotificationEventInput = {
  /**
   * Must match notification_event_type ENUM in DB.
   * Example: 'STUDENT_ABSENT'
   */
  type: string;

  /**
   * ID of the entity that triggered the event.
   * Example:
   * - attendance_id
   * - announcement_id
   * - test_id
   * - user_id (onboarding)
   */
  entityId: string;

  /**
   * Institute boundary for strict multi-tenant isolation.
   */
  instituteId: string;

  /**
   * Optional metadata used by dispatch layer
   * for recipient resolution or message formatting.
   */
  metadata?: Record<string, any>;
};

router.post("/login", async (req, res) => {
  const { login_identifier, password } = req.body;

  if (!login_identifier || !password) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      error: "login_identifier and password are required",
    });
  }

  const authResult = await authenticateUser(
    login_identifier,
    password
  );

  if (!authResult) {
    return res.status(401).json({
      error: "Invalid credentials",
    });
  }

  const sessionId = createSessionId();

  await createUserSession({
    sessionId,
    userId: authResult.user_id,
    expiresAt: getTokenExpiryDate(),
  });

  const accessToken = generateToken({
    ...authResult,
    session_id: sessionId,
  });

  const absoluteExpiresAt = getRefreshTokenAbsoluteExpiry(new Date());

  const { tokenValue: refreshTokenValue, expiresAt: refreshExpiresAt } =
    await createRefreshToken({
      userId: authResult.user_id,
      sessionId,
      familyId: null, // new login = new family
      absoluteExpiresAt,
    });

  // Refresh token lives in HttpOnly cookie — never accessible to JS
  res.cookie("refresh_token", refreshTokenValue, {
    httpOnly: true,
    secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === "production",
    sameSite: "strict",
    path: "/refresh",
    expires: refreshExpiresAt,
  });

  return res.status(200).json({
    token: accessToken,
    user: {
      user_id: authResult.user_id,
      role_id: authResult.role_id,
      institute_id: authResult.institute_id,
    },
  });
});


// POST /refresh — issues a new access token using the refresh token cookie
// This route does NOT require auth middleware (the access token may be expired)
router.post("/refresh", async (req, res) => {
  const refreshTokenValue: string | undefined = req.cookies?.refresh_token;

  if (!refreshTokenValue) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: "No refresh token provided" });
  }

  try {
    const rotated = await rotateRefreshToken(refreshTokenValue);

    if (!rotated) {
      // Token invalid, expired, already used, or replay detected
      res.clearCookie("refresh_token", {
        httpOnly: true,
        secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === "production",
        sameSite: "strict",
        path: "/refresh",
      });
      return res.status(401).json({ error: "Invalid or expired refresh token" });
    }

    // Fetch current user context for the new access token
    const userResult = await pool.query(
      `SELECT id, role_id, institute_id
       FROM "user"
       WHERE id = $1 AND is_active = true
       LIMIT 1`,
      [rotated.userId]
    );

    if (userResult.rowCount === 0) {
      res.clearCookie("refresh_token", {
        httpOnly: true,
        secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === "production",
        sameSite: "strict",
        path: "/refresh",
      });
      return res.status(401).json({ error: "User not found or inactive" });
    }

    const user = userResult.rows[0];

    const newAccessToken = generateToken({
      user_id: user.id,
      role_id: user.role_id,
      institute_id: user.institute_id,
      session_id: rotated.sessionId,
    });

    // Set the new rotated refresh token cookie
    res.cookie("refresh_token", rotated.newTokenValue, {
      httpOnly: true,
      secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === "production",
      sameSite: "strict",
      path: "/refresh",
      expires: rotated.newExpiresAt,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ token: newAccessToken });
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("[refresh] Error:", err?.message ?? err);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: "Token refresh failed" });
  }
});


router.use(requireAuth);

router.post("/logout", async (req, res) => {
  const context = (req as AuthenticatedRequest).context;

  await revokeUserSession({
    sessionId: context.session_id,
    userId: context.user_id,
  });

  await revokeRefreshTokensForSession(context.session_id);

  // Clear the refresh token cookie
  res.clearCookie("refresh_token", {
    httpOnly: true,
    secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === "production",
    sameSite: "strict",
    path: "/refresh",
  });

  return res.status(200).json({ message: "Logged out successfully" });
});
